<Review>This place reminds me of my childhood,Friday night pizza with my siblings! Featuring a brick wall, checkered table mats, blackboard walls with stylish writing on it (the menu) a semi open kitchen, (90‚Äôs style) soda fountain and even an old skool (sit down) 80‚Äôs arcade game!
As for the pizza itself: they do pizza by the slice here which I appreciate. Heavy cheese that‚Äôs distributed more from the center and less near the crust. I like the pizza here a lot I only mention criticism for aficionados. Somewhat typical ‚ÄúNew York style‚Äù I see around la but less big and less thin. I can tell they use very good ingredients. They don‚Äôt seem to be trying to do anything radically new or different but that‚Äôs kind of what you would want from a place like this.

The staff was really polite and seemed friendly.

The price point is very good. (For the area especially) $3.00 piece of cheese, not absurdly big but big enough to feel I got my money‚Äôs worth. If the slice was bigger I would make it a point to come back again and again. For now I would pick Roccos over most other places in the area.
I like the 90‚Äôs ninja turtle vibe, the price is good, the quality of pizza is rather good. It has a homey feel to it. Definitely a solid place to have a work meeting at.

Definitely business meeting and also sports bar vibe.< /Review>< Pics>

<Time>1508039161659< /Time>< rating>
5</rating>
< Text>
This would have been a 3 star review, but thanks to stellar customer service (on behalf of our server, John) I couldn't be quicker to change my mind. This was my uncle and I's first visit here and despite being avid restaurant goers, we don't usually bother leaving reviews.

We ordered a large pizza with several toppings, including bacon. It came out undercooked and rubbery which is a "no-go" for my uncle and I. When we brought it to John's attention, he couldn't be more responsive and accommodating. We suggested maybe that he take the bacon that was on the pizza and cook it longer as a means of being more reasonable, but he insisted they make it right and make a new one. He even insisted we keep the 1st pizza for our inconvenience which, even with no bacon, was DELICIOUS! It wasn't too doughy, the ingredients were fresh and they were very generous with the toppings.

We go out to eat almost all the time and we have experienced so many businesses that never bother to weigh to cost of repeat business vs bottom line. I would be thanking my lucky stars as a business owner in an economic climate like this to have an employee like John on their staff to look out for both the business AND the customers alike.

We will most certainly be eating here again and if you value the things I've written above, you ought to as well.< /Text>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
I work down the street from this place so it has become a frequent lunch spot for me and coworkers.  Not only is this place delicious but they have a great lunch special.  You can either get two slices of pizza, one topping each, and a soda or one slice of pizza, also one topping, with a salad and a drink for $7.  I always go with the latter so I don't feel so bad about my diet, especially when the slices are enormous.

We've never had a problem finding a table here, even when we come with a large party.  The staff is very friendly and don't hesitate to ask for suggestions or for something made especially for you.  If you're in the area and want some pretty good pizza for a cheap price then I recommend checking this place out.  I have yet to have a bad experience here and I always look forward to my next visit.</review>

< text>
This office is my distribution center and it's a nightmare. Our mail is delivered intermittently, which is to say, sometimes weeks go by with nothing or only one or two things, and then suddenly, all of our mail shows up, postmarked with dates 3 and 4 weeks previous. I've almost lost 4 packages because they haven't been delivered, and neither have the alert slips telling me to pick them up-or the follow up slips. In the first case, I had bought a package from an international vendor, and it was only when the vendor sent a message asking how I liked it that I realized it was supposed to be here. They kindly sent me the tracking info they'd had from their side and I found out it had been languishing for two and a half weeks with no notice whatsoever. I called, and of course, no one picked up the phone, which appears to be par for course at this location. I have *never* gotten through. So I called the USPS general number to find out how to get the package without a slip and they verified that it appeared the package was probably still around but close to the date of disposal (!) despite the fact that I had not as yet received a single notice.

So I went to the post office, armed with the package number I had received from the lovely woman on the USPS phone line. The desk staff were incredibly rude and impatient, but after waiting in a corner after explaining the situation as nicely as I could and somehow being treated as if I was at fault for not having a slip that had never been delivered in the first place, the staff person showed up with TWO packages. Apparently, two weeks earlier ANOTHER package had arrived, for which they had ALSO never sent any notice.

For weeks, mail service will be a little spotty but mostly reliable, if slow, and then these things will happen, often in a spate. I've even had packages ordered in the mail marked as "delivered" by the USPS which don't actually arrive until 2-5 days later. About 2 months ago, I had another package from a friend in MA take 4 weeks to get here, for no apparent reason, and currently, I have two packages, one from Amazon and another from a different vendor, shipped through FedEx, which, because our building is difficult to get into, apparently were fobbed off to the local USPS according to their respective tracking infos, both of them two weeks ago, and haven't been seen or heard from since, though they're marked as delivered. In the meantime, no mail has shown in my box for 4 days.

I am literally having packages mailed to friends in other zip codes now to avoid this nightmare. I honestly don't understand how this location is being run so terribly. I've never had an experience with a post office like this.<//text>

<Rate>4</Rate>< review>
UPDATE:
Tried this place again on a Tuesday. It was not busy, we were seated immediately and got helped pretty quick. Service was a lot better since it wasn't busy, sushi was flavorful and fresh. Its was a lot better than my last visit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The sushi here was just okay. Flavor was a bit plain compared to other AYCE sushi. I felt like this location needed more texture as most of there rolls seem mushy, plain and not flavorful. The albacore with the crispy onions on top was the only one I liked. They give you a small dessert (green tea, if you asked) but, gave it to me in a really broke plastic dish and ended up not eating it. Like how do you serve this to your customer!?

Service here was horrible as we did come in on a Tuesday and it was busy. The table next to us was seated after us and got served food immediately like 4 times. Our food took a while to come & refill other than water wouldn't come around as so often (I had just hot water w/lemon).

Overall, we were patient and just wanted to enjoy ourselves for dinner that night. Left the girls a nice tip but, that would probably be my first and last time there.< /review>

< Review>
This is a new AYCE sushi restaurant that we heard good things about, and boy was it good! This place is just down the street from our main sushi spot Hikari and we wanted to see how it stacked up. As far as AYCE places usually go, the fish had the best temperature, texture, and taste. The fish to rice ratio was just right, not too much or too little of anything. The selection of sushi is not as extensive as other places but the selection they do have is top notch quality.

The only knock I can give them is that a few of their rolls and nigiri are just drenched with whatever sauce comes with them. Not a big problem,I can just ask for less sauce on them.

All in all, very surprised. The location is hidden away behind a gym which worries me because I hope it doesn't close down on account  of the location like the other businesses before them. I'll definitely help them out by coming as often as me and my wallet allows!</Review>

<user>109348198617511642816</user><name>Doris Yunda< /name><Date>1568604366536<//Date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
This ice cream shop sells the best ice cream I have ever tasted in my life! It is made with fresh, high quality ingredients. The portions are SUPER generous and the prices are cheap. You won't find ice cream like this anywhere else.  If you like super sweet ice cream this place isn't for you though.  The sweetness level is just enough and it doesn't overpower any of the other ingredients.  I had the nut variety flavor and it had full chunks of real pecans, walnuts,  peanuts. I found a piece of heaven in this ice cream shop!< /Text>

< text>
This was my first time axe-throwing and I was honestly very surprised to have an amazing experience!
My two biggest concerns before coming here were [1] Lack of outdoor space as this place seemed indoors from the pictures and [2] potentially heavy weight axes would mean that this experience would soon get tiring!

I‚Äôm happy that both of my concerns turned out to be false alarms! While this place is partially indoors, they‚Äôve opened up the doors on both sides thereby allowing plenty of air circulation. Also, you can be masked while throwing the axes thereby making this a safe experience!

With regards to the axes, they have a pretty huge selection of axes ranging from lightweight to moderate and then the more heavier ones! Surprisingly none of the axes were as heavy and once our trainers taught us the right technique, it was smooth sailing from there!

In terms of logistics, there‚Äôs plenty of parking available. Besides axe throwing, you can also order drinks and beers. It‚Äôs worth noting that all slots start and stop at the same time and are 1:15 hours long ! If you‚Äôre certain that you‚Äôre not gonna be able to make it in time for your reservation, I‚Äôd call the place up and try to reschedule instead of coming in midway through your slot.

Highly highly recommend this experience especially with a larger group of friends !< /text>

<response>None< /response><Rate>5</Rate>< pics>
None<//pics>
<gmap_id>0x80d959cf8b07bcc1:0xb69a741609cdf68d< /gmap_id>< Text>
What wonderful home cooking, and such nice people. Syria is famous in the Arab world for its food. And this restaurant reflects that. I had a super delicious falafel, rolled in flat bread (not stuffed in Pita), and it fulfilled all my dreams. First and foremost, the falafels themselves were moist, flavorful,  and had the fragrance and taste of mild spices like Coriander, not overwhelmed by too much cumin. There was the perfect ratio of tomato, lettuce, cucumber, pickle and tahina, and i think i tasted some parsley in there. The last time I can remember truly being this happy with falafel was a family run Palestinian place in San Francisco, 19th St. Inner Sunset, 1992, where the owner's grandfather introduced me patiently to the great's of modern Arab music in the days of cassettes.

I also got hummus, mashed eggplant salad, stuffed grape leaves, and kibbeh take away, all of which were excellent as well. Also got two things I did not catch the name of, one a lovely milky pudding desert, the other savory rice and peas inside a baked filo dough that had the taste of butter and also pistachio, unusual and very very good.  Found some good prices on some groceries, too. Two thumbs up!

This is a small place with enough tables, and even though not fancy is still very pleasant, in part b/c of the very nice owners, from Syria and Nebraska, respectively.  I cant wait to go back!<//Text>

The wonderful employees at dutch brothers always make my day. everyone is just so nice, and they make our drinks extra sweet how I like! My wife Karen used to get the double chocolate mocha.  We used to drive through a couple times a week, but it's just been me lately. I miss her more and more every day. I still keep a little picture of her in my car, and I know she's here in spirit. We used to love morning trips for coffee, but it's been hard lately. I still order a drink for her, extra sweet how she likes. I can't bear being without her. I can't even throw away the cups. What the hell is wrong with me. We lost her last month and it doesn't feel real. Sometimes when the loneliness is too much ill sit with her picture and drink my morning coffee, have a little banter about the weather and pretend she isn't gone, just like the old days. I can feel her with me and that's all i need to keep me sane. I wish i could see her again, but death is the only thing that could bring us close again.
